# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5502
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5502
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5502
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5502 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5502 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5502 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5502 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5502 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5502 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Special CI recreation of China
character_event = {
	id = soh.5503
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = recreating_china
		copy_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5504 } # Inform the world
	}
}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = liao_founding
			}
		}
		
		name = REROLL # Maybe something else...
	}
	
	after = {
		clear_all_random_chinese_dynasty_names_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
				}
			}
			repeat_event = { id = soh.5505 } # Generate new names
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5506 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
						NOT = {
							has_opinion_modifier = {
								who = ROOT
								modifier = breakaway_pretender
							}
						}
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5506 } # Inform the world
			}
			event_target:new_eoc = {
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5507 } # Inform the EoC
			}
			event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_landed = yes
					}
					narrative_event = { id = soh.5508 } # Inform the former EoC, if relevant
				}
			}
			event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5508 } # Inform the former EoC's heir, if relevant
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5506
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5506
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5506
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5506 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5506 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5506 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_large_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5506 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5506 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5506 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

##### Inheritance of pretender empire

# Hidden setup
character_event = {
	id = soh.5509
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		FROMFROM = {
			save_event_target_as = old_pretender_emperor
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_feudal = yes
					is_landed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						NOT = {
							title = FROM
						}
						OR = {
							title = e_china # Special case: Destroy the pretender empire
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire # Special case: Destroy the pretender empire
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = soh.5599 } # Destroy the pretender empire
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				}
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
						has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5510 } # Wrong culture - convert?
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
						has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes # If you've got some weird culture, you don't get the choice
						controls_religion = no
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5511 } # Wrong culture - convert?
				}
				else = {
					narrative_event = { id = soh.5513 } # You are no longer Chinese Imperial
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				character_event = { id = soh.5515 } # Remain a pretender?
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5519 } # You are no longer Chinese Imperial
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						which = FROMFROM
					}
					update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5613 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
			else = {
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5615 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inherited pretender from the same dynasty - ineligible for Chinese Imperial due to culture - convert?
character_event = {
	id = soh.5510
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5510
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5510 # I will change my culture!
		
		culture = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					culture_group = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5510 # I would rather stop being Chinese Imperial...
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		prestige = 100
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5512 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = ambitious
				e_china = {
					OR = {
						has_holder = no
						holder_scope = {
							OR = {
								NOT = {
									government = chinese_imperial_government
								}
								has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
								has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inherited pretender from the same dynasty - ineligible for Chinese Imperial due to religion - convert?
character_event = {
	id = soh.5511
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5511
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
				true_religion = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5511 # I will change my religion!
		
		religion = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					culture_group = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5511 # I would rather stop being Chinese Imperial...
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		piety = 100
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5512 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				true_religion = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = cynical
				e_china = {
					OR = {
						has_holder = no
						holder_scope = {
							OR = {
								NOT = {
									government = chinese_imperial_government
								}
								has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
								has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 # One false faith is the same as any other...
				has_secret_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5514 } # Inform the world
		}
	}

				factor = 0.1
				trait = ambitious
				e_china = {
					OR = {
						holder_scope = {
							OR = {
								NOT = {
									government = chinese_imperial_government
								}
								has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
								has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				e_china = {
					has_holder = no # FDaTK or similar
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = proud
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5517
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5517
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5517
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5517 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5517 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5517 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_large_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5517 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5517 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5517 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Inherited pretender from another dynasty - ineligible
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5519
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5519
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5519
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5519 # It was not meant to be!
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5520 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

##### Inheritance of China

# Hidden setup
character_event = {
	id = soh.5521
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		FROMFROM = {
			save_event_target_as = old_emperor_of_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_feudal = yes
					is_landed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5599 } # Destroy any secondary empires
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					e_china = {
						has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5522 } # Inform the new EoC
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					e_china = {
						has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = no
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5524 } # Select a dynasty name
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5526 } # New dynasty name selection
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5528 } # New dynasty name selection
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5530 } # Pretender takes over
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				character_event = { id = soh.5533 } # Pretender takes over
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH

				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes

			}

					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				character_event = { id = soh.5537 } # Pretender takes over
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					FROMFROM = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5539 } # Ineligible due to culture - convert?
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					FROMFROM = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					controls_religion = no
				}
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5540 } # Ineligible due to religion - convert?
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				}
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5542 } # Wholly ineligible
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5544 } # Wholly ineligible
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5662 } # Create new dynasty
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						which = FROMFROM
					}
					update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5617 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
			else = {
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5619 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
		}
	}
}

# Old EoC was non-CI, China has dynasty name, inherited by same dynasty non-pretender
character_event = {
	id = soh.5522
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5523 } # Inform the world
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5523 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new EoC
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5523
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5523
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5523
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5523 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5523 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5523 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5523 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5523 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5523 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}

		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5525
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5525
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5525
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5525 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5523 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5525 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5525 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5525 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5525 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5527 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5527 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5527
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5527
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5527
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5527 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5527 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5527 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_large_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5527 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5527 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5527 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

	after = {
		clear_all_random_chinese_dynasty_names_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
				}
			}
			repeat_event = { id = soh.5528 } # Generate new names
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5529 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5529 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5529
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5529
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5529
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5529 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5529 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5529 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5529 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5529 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM

# Old EoC was CI, inherited by same dynasty pretender
character_event = {
	id = soh.5530
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5530
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5530 # I will end the pretender dynasty!
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5531 } # Inform the world
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5531 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = proud
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5530 # I will keep the pretender dynasty!
		
		copy_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5532 } # Inform the world
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5532 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world that the pretender kept the same dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5531
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5531
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5531
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5531 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5531 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5531 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5531 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5531 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5531 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Inherited China from the same dynasty - ineligible for Chinese Imperial due to culture - convert?
character_event = {
	id = soh.5539
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5539
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5539 # I will change my culture!
		
		culture = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					culture_group = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5539 # I would rather stop being Chinese Imperial...
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		prestige = 100
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes # Clear out Grace and Chinese Princesses
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5541 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = ambitious
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inherited China from the same dynasty - ineligible for Chinese Imperial due to religion - convert?
character_event = {
	id = soh.5540
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5540
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
				true_religion = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5540 # I will change my religion!
		
		religion = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					culture_group = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5540 # I would rather stop being Chinese Imperial...
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		piety = 100
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes # Clear out Grace and Chinese Princesses
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5541 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				true_religion = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 # One false faith is the same as any other...
				has_secret_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

##### Usurpation of pretender

# Hidden setup
character_event = {
	id = soh.5546
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		NOR = {
			has_landed_title = e_china # Special case
			any_demesne_title = {
				NOT = {
					title = FROM
				}
				has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire # Special case
			}
			has_character_flag = special_chinse_imperial_usurpation
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		FROMFROM = {
			save_event_target_as = old_pretender_emperor
			add_trait = former_eoc_trait
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_feudal = yes
					is_landed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				}
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = FROMFROM
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
						has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5547 } # Wrong culture - convert?
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
						has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes # If you've got some weird culture, you don't get the choice
						controls_religion = no
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5548 } # Wrong culture - convert?
				}
				else = {
					narrative_event = { id = soh.5550 } # You are no longer Chinese Imperial
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = FROMFROM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5552 } # Do you want to keep being a pretender?
				}
				else = {
					narrative_event = { id = soh.5556 } # You are no longer Chinese Imperial
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						which = FROMFROM
					}
					mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
					update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5621 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
			else = {
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5623 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

				}

				factor = 0

					has_holder = no # FDaTK or similar
				}
			}

# If still a pretender, select a dynasty name
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5553
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5553
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5553
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	immediate = {
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
			clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
		}
		generate_three_random_chinese_dynasty_names_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = ba_china_option
		}
		
		name = BA
		
		primary_title = {
			set_title_flag = ba_china
			set_global_flag = ba_china_exists
			set_short_name = no
			set_name = "Ba"
			adjective = "Ba"
		}
		
		set_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			ba_china_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = bei_china_option
		}
		
		name = BEI
		
		primary_title = {
			set_title_flag = bei_china
			set_global_flag = bei_china_exists
			set_short_name = no
			set_name = "Bei"
			adjective = "Bei"
		}
		
		set_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			bei_china_score = yes

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5554
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5554
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5554
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5554 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
				NOT = {
					character = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5554 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5554 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_large_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_pretender_emperor
			}
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5554 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5554 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5554 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes

		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5557 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

##### Usurpation of China

# Hidden start
character_event = {
	id = soh.5558
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		FROMFROM = {
			save_event_target_as = old_emperor_of_china
			add_trait = former_eoc_trait
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5559 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5560 } # If the old EoC wasn't CI, they don't suffer certain penalties
		}
	}
}

# Old EoC informed of loss of tributaries, duchies, and kingdoms
character_event = {
	id = soh.5559
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5559
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5559 # This keeps getting worse...
		
		china_usurpation_effect = yes # Transfer the de jure capital, destroy duchies and kingdoms of old EoC, downgrade tributaries of old EoC and usurp them
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5560 } # Determine further fallout
		}
	}
}

# Ping EoC and do the setup
character_event = {
	id = soh.5560
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_feudal = yes
					is_landed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						tier = emperor
						NOT = {
							title = e_china
						}
					}
					unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
					add_pressed_claim = PREV
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
						has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
						event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
							can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5561 } # Wrong culture - convert?
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
						has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes # If you've got some weird culture, you don't get the choice
						controls_religion = no
					}
					character_event = { id = soh.5562 } # Wrong culture - convert?
				}
				else = {
					narrative_event = { id = soh.5564 } # You are no longer Chinese Imperial!
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5566 } # You are no longer Chinese Imperial!
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					e_china = {
						has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5568 } # No need to rename China
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					e_china = {
						has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = no
					}
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5570 } # Need to rename China
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5572 } # Need to rename China
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5574 } # Keep pretender dynasty?
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
					}
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				# Transfer MoH
				change_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				character_event = { id = soh.5577 } # Keep pretender dynasty
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = emperor
						has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				character_event = { id = soh.5579 } # Keep pretender dynasty
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						has_character_flag = china_usurper_claimant_faction_or_takeover
					}
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5581 } # Need to rename China
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					has_character_flag = china_usurper_claimant_faction_or_takeover
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = emperor
							has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
						}
					}
				}
				set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
				clr_character_flag = china_usurper_claimant_faction_or_takeover
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5583 } # Need to rename China... and could possibly result in interesting times
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						which = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
					update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5625 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
			else = {
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5627 } # You are ineligible due to being non-feudal!
			}
		}
	}
}

# Usurped China from the same dynasty - ineligible for Chinese Imperial due to culture
character_event = {
	id = soh.5561
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5561
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5561 # I will change my culture!
		
		culture = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					culture_group = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5561 # I would rather stop being Chinese Imperial...
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		prestige = 100
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes # Clear out Grace and Chinese Princesses
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5563 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = ambitious
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new EoC
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5569
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5569
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5569
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5569 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5569 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5569 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5569 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5569 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5569 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

		}

	after = {
		clear_all_random_chinese_dynasty_names_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
				}
			}
			repeat_event = { id = soh.5570 } # Generate new names
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5571 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5571 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5571
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5571
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5571
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5571 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5571 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5571 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5571 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5571 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5571 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

	after = {

		}

			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5573 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5573 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5573
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5573
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5573
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5573 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5573 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5573 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5573 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5573 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Same dynasty pretender took over China from CI EoC - keep the dynasty name?
character_event = {
	id = soh.5574
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5574
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5574 # I will end the pretender dynasty!
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5575 } # Inform the world
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5575 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = proud
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5574 # I will keep the pretender dynasty!
		
		copy_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5576 } # Inform the world
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5576 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the same dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5575
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5575
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5575
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5575 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5575 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5575 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}

		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}

			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5576 # Ten thousand years!
	}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}

				limit = {
					NOT = {

					}

			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}

				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}

			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china

		}
	}

			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}

	}

				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5576 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {

		}
		
		set_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			zou_china_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
		
		name = REROLL # Maybe something else...
	}
	
	after = {
		clear_all_random_chinese_dynasty_names_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
				}
			}
			repeat_event = { id = soh.5581 } # Generate new names
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5582 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5582 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5582
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5582
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5582
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5582 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5582 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5582 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5582 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5582 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5582 # This does not concern me...
	}
}
