# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5584
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5584
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5584
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5584 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5584 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5584 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5584 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5584 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5584 # This does not concern me...
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:new_eoc
				event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					name = chinese_implosion
					value = allowed
				}
			}
			event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5634 } # Let the interesting times begin!
			}
		}
	}
}



##### Religion/culture conversion affecting status as CI

# Pretender converted culture - no longer Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = soh.5585
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5585
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		primary_title = {
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		FROM = {
			has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5585 # It was not meant to be!
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5586 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world - pretender no longer Chinese Imperial due to culture
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5586
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5586
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5586
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5586 # FROM was only a false dragon!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5586 # Interesting...
	}
}

# Pretender converted religion - no longer Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = soh.5587
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5587
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		primary_title = {
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		FROM = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5587 # It was not meant to be!
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5588 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# EoC converted culture - no longer Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = soh.5589
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5589
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		has_landed_title = e_china
		FROM = {
			has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5589 # It was not meant to be!
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes # Clear out Grace and Chinese Princesses
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5590 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age

	is_triggered_only = yes

		has_landed_title = e_china
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		FROM = {
			has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		religion = buddhist # Only relevant religion
		e_china = {
			has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
		}
		is_feudal = yes
	}
	
	option = {

				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5598 } # Inform the world
		}

		}

			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5598 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5598 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}

# Inform the world - China is now CI
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5598
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5598
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5598
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5598 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5598 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5598 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5598 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5598 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5598 # This does not concern me...
	}
}



##### Misc

# Destroy any secondary empires gained by a CI ruler (except China itself) outside special circumstances
character_event = {
	id = soh.5599
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
				is_primary_holder_title = no
			}
			clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Alternative triggering of soh.5599 from various on_new_holder on_actions
character_event = {
	id = soh.5600
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = chinese_imperial_government
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
			NOR = {
				title = e_china
				has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = soh.5599 } # Destroy the title
	}
}

# Yearly cleanup of flags and names for titles without holders

	id = soh.5601
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	religion = catholic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		controls_religion = yes # The Pope is always around!
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clean_up_all_chinese_pretenders_effect = yes
	}
}

# Cleanup of dynasty name if non-CI China is taken over by non-CI ruler
character_event = {
	id = soh.5602
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
		}
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		e_china = {
			has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes # Clear out Grace and Chinese Princesses
		e_china = {
			clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# on_startup, add the eoc_trait to all CI rulers
character_event = {
	id = soh.5603
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	religion = catholic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		controls_religion = yes # The Pope is always around!
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = eoc_trait_added
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = eoc_trait_added
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					primary_title = { has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire }
					has_landed_title = e_china
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
			primary_title = {
				update_global_china_flags_effect = yes # Make sure dynasties are properly tracked
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_1
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					duration = -1
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					value = -90
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_1
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Lost!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_2
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					duration = -1
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					value = -50
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_2
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Poor!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_3
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					duration = -1
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					value = 0
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_3
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Average!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_4
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					duration = -1
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					value = 50
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_4
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Good!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_5
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					duration = -1
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					value = 90
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_5
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Unquestioned!"
			}
			else = {
				set_character_flag = fallback_starting_mandate_set
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating will use the fallback option!"
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					duration = -1
				}
				clr_character_flag = moh_3
			}
			add_trait = eoc_trait
			character_event = { id = soh.5301 } # Generate starting Court Eunuchs
		}
	}
}

# Clean up extra empires if suddenly Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = soh.5604
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		e_china = {
			make_primary_title = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
				NOT = {
					title = e_china
				}
			}
			unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			add_pressed_claim = PREV
		}
	}
}

# on_death event to set temple names
character_event = {
	id = soh.5605
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = 1051151 ### Song Dynasty, known in almost all official artwork as wearing their weird zhangokfutou
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = song_china # If someone creates a "Song", give them the proper headgear!
					}
				}
			}
			add_trait = dead_song_emperor # Complimentary zhangokfutou
		}
					
		# Historical EoCs (that held e_china) get their historical temple name
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_daizong
			}
			set_name = "Daizong"
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_dezong
			}
			set_name = "Dezong"
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_shunzong
			}
			set_name = "Shunzong"
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_xianzong
			}
			set_name = "Xianzong"
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_muzong

##### Mandate of Heaven

# on_yearly_pulse - update the MoH
character_event = {
	id = soh.5607
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		calculate_mandate_of_heaven_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world - triggered from MoH update
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5608
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5608
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	major_trigger = {
		ai = no
		OR = {
			is_within_diplo_range = event_target:mandate_update_character
			top_liege = {
				OR = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_A
		picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_B
		picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_C
		picture = GFX_evt_china_stable
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_D
		picture = GFX_evt_china_unrest
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_E
		picture = GFX_evt_china_civil_war
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = event_target:mandate_update_character
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			top_liege = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			government = chinese_imperial_government
		}
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					character = event_target:mandate_update_character
				}
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			independent = no
		}
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				any_realm_province = {
					OR = {
						trade_route = silk_road
						region = world_china
						county = {
							de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
}

# on_tyranny_gained_tyrant_only event hurting MoH

	only_independent = yes

# on_death handling of viceroyalties if the liege has a special succession law
character_event = {
	id = soh.5610
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			is_vice_royalty = yes
			tier = king
		}
		liege = {
			primary_title = {
				OR = {
					has_law = chinese_succession
					has_law = ma_chu
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				is_vice_royalty = yes
				tier = king
			}
			set_title_flag = should_change_succession_law
		}
	}
}

# on_new_holder_inheritance handling of the above
character_event = {
	id = soh.5611
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_title_flag = should_change_succession_law
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			clr_title_flag = should_change_succession_law
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = chinese_succession
						}
					}
				}
				add_law = {
					law = chinese_succession
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = ma_chu
						}
					}
				}
				add_law = {
					law = ma_chu
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Handle titles usurped from vassals on_new_holder_usurpation
character_event = {
	id = soh.5612
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		real_tier = emperor
		FROM = {
			tier = king
		}
		primary_title = {
			OR = {
				has_law = chinese_succession
				has_law = ma_chu
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = chinese_succession
						}
					}
				}
				add_law = {
					law = chinese_succession
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = ma_chu
						}
					}
				}
				add_law = {
					law = ma_chu
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}



##### Handling of non-feudal (is_feudal = no) inheritance/usurpation

# Non-feudal ruler inherited pretender from the same dynasty - ineligible
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5613
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5613
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5613
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5613 # It was not meant to be!
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5614 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# Non-feudal ruler usurped China from other dynasty - ineligible
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5627
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5627
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5627
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5627 # It was not meant to be!
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5628 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

##### Handling of tribals converting to feudalism while holding China

# Became feudal when holding China - China named - EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5629
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5629
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = e_china
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		FROM = {
			has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		religion = buddhist # Only relevant religion
		e_china = {
			has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
		}
		is_feudal = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5629 # Ten thousand years!
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		character_event = { id = soh.5604 } # Destroy other empires
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5630 } # Inform the world
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5630 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world - China is once more Chinese Imperial
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5630
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5630
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5630
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5630 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		}
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5630 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5630 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5630 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5630 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5630 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

		if = {

			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5633 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5633 } # Inform the world

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5633
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5633
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5633
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5633 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5633 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5633 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5633 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5633 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5633 # This does not concern me...
	}
}



##### Special FDaTK-style outcome - TODO: AI logic

# TODO: Handle permanent regents; they should always follow their liege, if relevant
# General ideas for the AI logic:
# - Kings never stay vassals of either side unless from the same dynasty and with a suitable culture + religion
# - Rel heads always break free from non-co-religionist liege
# - Former faction backers (check opinion modifiers) side with the guy they backed
# - If not eligible for ConBu or CI, always break free
# - Dynasty members generally side with the dynasty, rarely break free
# - Traits should matter a lot; Ambitious kings should be more likely to claim the Mandate than Content ones, etc.
# - Friends and lovers likely side with friend/lover, rivals likely side against, barring very compelling reasons
# - If the mandate_of_heaven_x modifier of the new EoC is higher than that of the former dynasty, be more likely to side with that, and the other way around
# - Don't side with someone you consider a tyrant
# - Opinion matters; barring compelling reasons, > 50 opinion should probably convince someone to side with that person, < -50 should probably convince someone to side against that person
# - Independence faction members are unlikely to remain vassals

# Hidden setup to determine which version we get
character_event = {
	id = soh.5634
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
				has_regent = no
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				is_adult = yes
				# Capable of ruling
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5635 } # Do you want to create a pretender
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_dynasty_member = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					top_liege = {
						character = event_target:new_eoc
					}
					is_playable = yes
					is_feudal = yes
					has_regent = no
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_adult = yes
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					# Capable of ruling
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5645 } # See if a dynasty member wishes to create a pretender
		}
		else = {
			event_target:new_eoc = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5658 } # See what the realm lords do
			}
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC is still able to govern (not imprisoned/a child/etc.) - do they want to create a pretender?
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5635
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5635
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5635
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5635 # My dynasty is the only legitimate dynasty!
		
		any_realm_lord = {
			limit = {
				higher_tier_than = baron
			}
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			set_defacto_liege = event_target:new_eoc
		}
		any_war = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					attacker = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					defender = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
		}
		set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		give_random_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = continue_same_dynasty
			name_pretender_after_old_china_effect = yes
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = breakaway_pretender
			}
		}
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = breakaway_pretender
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					character = event_target:new_eoc
					NOT = {
						top_liege = {
							character = event_target:new_eoc
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5636 } # Inform the world
		}
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5637 } # Ping, then go to vassals
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5635 # I have lost the Mandate of Heaven!
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5637 } # Ping, then go to vassals
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC broke away - inform the world
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5636
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5636
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5636
	picture = GFX_evt_china_civil_war
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = event_target:new_eoc
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5636 # Didn't you already learn your lesson?
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:new_eoc
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5636 # I am the true Emperor of China!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5636 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5636 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Ping new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5637
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_realm_lord = {
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					is_patrician = no
				}
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT # To avoid sub-vassals going with a liege they shouldn't go with
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
					has_regent = no
					OR = {
						is_patrician = no
						is_merchant_republic = yes
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5638 } # Make a decision
			}
		}
	}
}

# Count+ ream lords that aren't patricians get to make a choice to back either side, go independent, or maybe even go pretender
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5638
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5638
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5638
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5638 # I will remain loyal to the new Son/Daughter of Heaven!
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5639 } # Inform EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5640 } # Inform former EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = {
					dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5638 # I will remain loyal to the old Son/Daughter of Heaven!
		
		set_defacto_liege = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5641 } # Inform EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5642 } # Inform former EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOR = {
					dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				can_have_confucian_bureaucracy_and_eastern_imperial_trigger = no
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5638 # Neither of them is worthy of my allegiance!
		
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5643 } # Inform EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5644 } # Inform former EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_feudal = yes
			real_tier = king
			NOR = {
				dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
				dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5638 # Actually, the Mandate of Heaven belongs to ME!
		
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		give_random_pretender_empire_with_chinas_laws_effect = yes
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = breakaway_pretender
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5505 } # Name the pretender empire
	}
}

# Remained loyal to the new EoC - inform new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5639
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5639
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_success
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5639 # Excellent!
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tier = king
				}
			}
			mandate_boost_large_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tier = duke
				}
			}
			mandate_boost_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			mandate_boost_small_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Loop over former EoC's dynasty member, as required
character_event = {
	id = soh.5645
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_dynasty_member = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					top_liege = {
						character = event_target:new_eoc
					}
					is_playable = yes
					is_feudal = yes
					has_regent = no
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_adult = yes
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					# Capable of ruling
					NOT = {
						has_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
					}
				}
			}
			random_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					top_liege = {
						character = event_target:new_eoc
					}
					is_playable = yes
					is_feudal = yes
					has_regent = no
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_adult = yes
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					# Capable of ruling
					NOT = {
						has_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
					}
				}
				preferred_limit = {
					ROOT = {
						current_heir = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				preferred_limit = {
					real_tier = king
				}
				preferred_limit = {
					real_tier = duke
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5646 } # Do you want to keep the dynasty going?
			}
		}
		else = {
			any_dynasty_member = {
				clr_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
			}
			event_target:new_eoc = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5658 } # See what the realm lords do
			}
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC is not able to govern but there's a dynasty member that could - do they want to create a pretender?
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5646
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5646
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5635
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5646 # My dynasty is the only legitimate dynasty!
		
		any_dynasty_member = {
			clr_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
		}
		
		any_realm_lord = {
			limit = {
				higher_tier_than = baron
			}
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			set_defacto_liege = event_target:new_eoc
		}
		any_war = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					attacker = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					defender = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
		}
		set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		save_event_target_as = old_emperor_of_china_heir
		give_random_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = continue_same_dynasty
			name_pretender_after_old_china_as_heir_effect = yes
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = breakaway_pretender
			}
		}
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = breakaway_pretender
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					character = event_target:new_eoc
					NOT = {
						top_liege = {
							character = event_target:new_eoc
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5647 } # Inform the world
		}
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5648 } # Ping, then go to vassals
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5646 # We have lost the Mandate of Heaven!
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		}
		set_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5645 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC's relative broke away - inform the world

	id = soh.5647

							county = {

						}
					}

			}
		}

					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM

						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5647 # This does not concern me...

# Ping new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5648
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_realm_lord = {
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					is_patrician = no
				}
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT # To avoid sub-vassals going with a liege they shouldn't go with
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
					OR = {
						has_regent = no
						character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
					OR = {
						is_patrician = no
						is_merchant_republic = yes
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5649 } # Make a decision
			}
		}
	}
}

# Count+ ream lords that aren't patricians get to make a choice to back either side, go independent, or maybe even go pretender; former EoC gets to abdicate to new pretender
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5649
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5649
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5649
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5649 # I will remain loyal to the new Son/Daughter of Heaven!
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5650 } # Inform EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5651 } # Inform former EoC's heir # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = {
					dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5649 # I will remain loyal to the old Son/Daughter of Heaven's dynasty!
		
		set_defacto_liege = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5652 } # Inform EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5653 } # Inform former EoC's heir # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOR = {
					dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
				can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				can_have_confucian_bureaucracy_and_eastern_imperial_trigger = no
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5649 # Neither of them is worthy of my allegiance!
		
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5654 } # Inform EoC # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5655 } # Inform former EoC's heir # TODO: Hide due to spam?
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_feudal = yes
			real_tier = king
			NOR = {
				dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
				dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5649 # Actually, the Mandate of Heaven belongs to ME!
		
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = claims_all_of_your_titles
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						add_weak_pressed_claim = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		give_random_pretender_empire_with_chinas_laws_effect = yes
		add_trait= eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = breakaway_pretender
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5505 } # Name the pretender empire
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5648 # I will give my full support to my heir!
		
		abdicate_to = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		add_trait = former_eoc_trait
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
			
		move_character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		force_host = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5656 } # Inform EoC
		}
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5657 } # Inform former EoC's heir
		}
	}
}

	id = soh.5650
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5650
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_success
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5650 # Excellent!
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tier = king
				}
			}
			mandate_boost_large_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tier = duke
				}
			}
			mandate_boost_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			mandate_boost_small_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Ping new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5658
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_realm_lord = {
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					is_patrician = no
				}
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT # To avoid sub-vassals going with a liege they shouldn't go with
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
					has_regent = no
					OR = {
						is_patrician = no
						is_merchant_republic = yes
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5659 } # Make a decision
			}
		}
	}
}

			set_title_flag = zhu_china
			set_global_flag = zhu_china_exists
			set_short_name = no
			set_name = "Zhu"
			adjective = "Zhu"
		}
		
		set_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			zhu_china_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = zhuan_china_option
		}
		
		name = ZHUAN
		
		primary_title = {
			set_title_flag = zhuan_china
			set_global_flag = zhuan_china_exists
			set_short_name = no
			set_name = "Zhuan"
			adjective = "Zhuan"
		}
		
		set_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			zhuan_china_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = zou_china_option
		}
		
		name = ZOU
		
		primary_title = {
			set_title_flag = zou_china
			set_global_flag = zou_china_exists
			set_short_name = no
			set_name = "Zou"
			adjective = "Zou"
		}
		
		set_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			zou_china_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
		
		name = REROLL # Maybe something else...
	}
	
	after = {
		clear_all_random_chinese_dynasty_names_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
				}
			}
			repeat_event = { id = soh.5662 } # Generate new names
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5663 } # Inform the world
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5663 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5663
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5663
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5663
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5663 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5663 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5663 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5663 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5663 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5663 # This does not concern me...
	}
}
